Commentary

It Is Both Theory and Fact Zhao Wenyuan 275

In the previous issues of this publication's special issue on female workers, there are two very obvious facts being manifested: one is the absolute or relative increase of female laborers in various industrial sectors, and the other is the absolute or relative decrease of male laborers in various industrial sectors, and the further fact that female laborers are driving male laborers out of all industrial sectors and implementing a monopoly over all labor sectors. This is a phenomenon unique to the current capitalist society, and there is no need for us to doubt it. As long as one examines the facts of the industrial revolution's evolution in various countries, it is not difficult to grasp the core of this issue.

The industrial revolution has made the greatest effort in the completion of capitalism. It is the death knell of the old society, and at the same time, it is the harbinger of the birth of the new society. It has simplified human labor, so that the manual labor required for spinning and weaving is mainly limited to connecting broken threads. Because all other labor is taken over by machines. Therefore, this labor does not require much effort, and only requires skillful movements with the fingers. In these simplified industrial sectors, female laborers can naturally work without needing much skill or strength. Therefore, those skilled and physically strong male laborers have reduced their original required area and are quickly squeezed out of their respective labor sectors. Moreover, the wages paid to female laborers are also very low. This fact of using cheap wages is even more beneficial to the capitalist class, which gains surplus value by reducing production costs. In this way, female laborers sweep everything away and monopolize all labor sectors.

The result of women monopolizing the labor market will at least cause the following repercussions. The first is that most or even all of the male laborers are squeezed out and roam the streets, forming a large industrial reserve army. The second is the reduction of labor value, so that the result of the laboring class working hard throughout the year is not enough to maintain their minimum standard of living, leading to widespread impoverishment. The third is that the mortality rate of children who leave their mothers, who must go to society to sell their labor, shows a sharp increase due to the lack of constant care. This phenomenon is being enacted very rapidly from England, the birthplace of the industrial revolution, to various colonial countries where industry has only recently developed. This is the most common phenomenon in the international community, and it is also a characteristic of the world's current physical state.

In order to prepare for a rainy day, our country, which is in this atmosphere, should, in the passive aspect, make it impossible for this phenomenon to be repeated in our country; and in the active aspect, begin to reform the social system that produces this phenomenon. We must ensure that every young man and woman has the opportunity to share labor and enjoy the benefits together, and never allow the biased phenomenon of men excluding women or women excluding men to appear in the labor world. Make all of human material civilization a source of public happiness, and do not let it become a shackle to the evolution of human society. This is the true meaning of human control of the material world.

Notes on the Daily Life of Heroes A Certain Manager

Broken Leather Shoes Ms. Xiang Ling 276

Ling, who graduated from high school but couldn't afford to go to college, stayed at home and brooded for two whole years. Later, thanks to a friend's introduction, he got a job as a junior clerk in a certain foreign firm.

Ling had suffered enough from the taste of being idle at home and the shame of being unemployed for two years. Now he actually ran briskly into the magnificent foreign firm on the road every day, unlike before when he ran on ordinary days, he used to avoid acquaintances in a fluster; the sad mood of the rice jar being empty at home in the past was also gone. Ling was as happy as all the young people who had just found a job, and he cherished many fantasies.

The manager was a tall American. Because he had always had a very comfortable life, he had grown fat and strong. One day, the manager suddenly asked Ling to take a pair of black leather shoes with broken soles to the cheapest shoe store for repair. The manager said, "The quality must be good, and the time must be fast. These shoes are genuine American goods, and it would be a pity to lose them."

Ling was very unhappy in his heart. Why didn't a dignified manager take his shoes to a foreign shoe store, but insisted on a Chinese person taking them to a Chinese store for repair? How meticulous he is! But these shoes are the manager's! So after using all his brainpower to compare the many shoe stores he knew in his heart, he finally took them to a shoe store that he thought was the most reliable. After agreeing on a price of two yuan, he instructed the clerk:

"These shoes belong to our manager. The quality must be good, and I'll pick them up the day after tomorrow!"

The third day arrived, but the manager didn't mention the shoes, nor did he give him the money to pick them up. Ling was already very anxious in his heart. That afternoon, he went to the shoe store on the way to work to pick up the shoes and bring them back to the firm.

The manager had already arrived at the firm. He was leaning back in a comfortable chair, reading a newspaper, with a large cigar in his mouth. Ling, carrying the shoes, strode into the magnificent manager's office, as if he had done something meritorious. The manager didn't move at all, but kept reading the newspaper. Ling tremblingly placed the shoes in front of the manager.

"Oh, goodll!" the manager called out, picked up the shoes and looked them over. Suddenly his face turned red, his eyes widened in anger, and he threw the shoes on the ground with a bang: "I don't want this kind of dog skin! Take it apart!"

Ling's heart was pounding, and his face turned pale. A burst of anger rushed to his heart. He wanted to scold this Westerner fiercely, then put on his hat and go home! But he didn't have that kind of courage. He finally bent down, picked up the shoes, and went to that shoe store again. Because his subconscious told him: his mother and younger brother were relying on him for this job to eat! He said to the shoe store clerk:

"I'm really sorry!：：：My manager is a pig! He said the leather wasn't good and wanted it taken apart. Please reduce the price a little bit. I'll pay for it myself. I'm just unlucky!"

That clerk was still polite and agreed to reduce the price by one yuan.

Ling seemed to have escaped a disaster as he carried the shoes back to the firm. He angrily placed the shoes on the manager's desk. The manager didn't say a word and didn't even look at Ling. The bills and invoices piled up on Ling's desk, and he,

Page 21

stared blankly at the typewriter, unable to concentrate on his work.

When he went home for dinner in the evening, his mother saw that he was silent and asked, "Ling, why do you look so unhappy tonight? Did the manager scold you?" "No, no," Ling replied quickly before he even swallowed a mouthful of rice, and tears almost flowed down.

Slum Dwellings

The Evening and Morning of a Junior Clerk 277

— Yi Niao

The Garret

After toiling in the company for a whole day, I returned to my dormitory in the evening: the garret. It was time to rest. I walked to the edge of the bed and sat down. After lying down for a while, I opened a literary work I had just bought yesterday. Just as I was engrossed in reading, a burst of laughter and talking suddenly entered my ears:

"One missing for mahjong!" It seemed to be the voice of the woman upstairs in the front. "Playing mahjong? I'm in!" said the woman upstairs in the back.

In no time, they started their work with "Pi! Pa!" This made me embarrassed. I read the book for a while and then went to turn it off. I pondered for a moment, looked at the alarm clock on the windowsill, and the short hand was pointing to half past nine. I thought, I'd better go to bed early, so as not to hear those annoying sounds. So I opened the blanket.

But the opposite was true. The sound of "Pi! Pa!" was even more distinct. This was terrible! If I put my head in the blanket, it would be unhygienic. But the sound of mahjong would not stop for a moment. There was no way out, so I had to bite the bullet and get into the blanket. This seemed better, but it was stuffy and difficult to breathe, very uncomfortable. Finally, I barely entered the land of dreams.

"Pong! Eat! Win!" Just as I was having a sweet dream, I was suddenly awakened by them. The reason was that my head was no longer in the blanket. I turned on the light, rubbed my eyes, and looked at the clock. It was already twelve o'clock. At this time, I became furious. It's already the middle of the night, and they're still not tired of playing. Don't they care that people need to sleep? The thought of "moving out" came to my mind again, but if I moved out, would I be able to completely avoid hearing the sound of mahjong? As I thought of this, there was another burst of children crying. I sighed deeply and got back into my blanket.

"Chacha chacha," suddenly a sound of dumping the chamber pot broke my sweet dream. I opened my drowsy eyes and looked out the window. A faint ray of sunlight had already shone on the corner of someone's house. At this time, the sound of mahjong in my ears changed to the "chacha" sound of the chamber pot.

I got up and put on my clothes, wanting to open the window to get some fresh air, but the disgusting stench had already rushed in. The "chacha" sound became even more intense. I couldn't open it, so I had to close it.

Ah! I don't even have the right to get fresh air. I went out to wash my face, and I had to press the abacus. After washing up, I walked out of my dormitory and stepped back into the company to struggle for life.

Evidence of Crime 278

— Jing Jia

I am a junior clerk in a company. I have to get to the company before seven o'clock every day, and I can't go home until it's dark. Sometimes I even have to work overtime.

The manager looks down on us. He doesn't allow us to take leave, and one day of leave will be deducted one day's pay. Even being half an hour late will be fined. The same goes for leaving early.

One day, I got up early and left without eating breakfast as usual. I live far away from the company, and I have to take a bus or tram.

I stood at the bus stop waiting for a long time, but I still didn't see the shadow of the bus. I was getting angry in my heart. At this time, the clock hand was already pointing to half past six. Finally, the bus came, but it was a reserved car. After a while, a bus full of passengers came, and even the door wouldn't open, no matter how much you shouted. Three buses passed in a row, and they were all like that.

It was already seven o'clock, but I was still standing at the bus stop. If I wanted to take a rickshaw, it would cost me forty cents, but my daily income is at most sixty cents. Alas, I really wanted to die at that time!

Finally, I arrived at the company at seven forty-five. The manager called me to go, and I knew that a scolding was unavoidable.

"Why are you late?" he said, "I've already arrived, and you're still not here?"

"I really couldn't get a bus," I answered in a low voice.

"Hmph, you never used to wait for the bus, but today you're waiting for the bus!"

This sentence was the evidence of my crime. This time, the punishment I received was not great, but I couldn't stand this grievance!

Alas, what should I do? Do I have to be their ox and horse, exhausting my spirit for them until I die?

Folk Anecdotes

The Struggle Before the Fall 280

— Ruo Zhou

This is a general rule. When everything is in the process of transition from old to new, the old things are never willing to die quietly. They always struggle, hoping that their lives will be prolonged unexpectedly. The closer they get to death, the more fierce their struggle becomes. In the last moment, they will even take out the most cruel, shameless, and at the same time, the most naive and ridiculous methods to fight with the new, trying to seize back their dying fate from this last gasp of struggle. But the facts ultimately do not allow them to do so. Everything, everything, is moving forward at all times. The universe is constantly running. The old is bound to die, and the new will eventually rise. No matter how desperately they struggle, the result is still in vain. Moreover, because of their excessive struggle, it will cause their accelerated collapse. Struggle or not, history never stays and never retreats.

I remember that when the revolutionary army started the Northern Expedition in the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, Sun Chuanfang, a warlord in Southeast China, although he hated the revolution, because the revolutionary army had not directly conflicted with his own interests for a while, although he had already imposed a kind of oppression on the revolutionary forces lurking under his rule, it was not very cruel. Newspapers in the Jiangsu and Zhejiang areas could still see records about the activities of the Kuomintang. Later, as the revolutionary army progressed steadily, it had occupied Jiangxi in a few months. Sun Chuanfang's rule was obviously shaken, and his fate was obviously declining day by day. So he began to make a fierce struggle and began to cruelly suppress the revolutionary forces. At that time, not to mention that the newspapers no longer saw records about the activities of the Kuomintang, as long as a copy of the Three Principles of the People was found in the bookshelf, it would be executed immediately. Even casually discussing the current situation was also in danger of being beheaded. Secret agents were everywhere along the Hu-Ning Road, and countless young people were killed for no reason. Li Baozhang, a well-known executioner, his broadsword team was even more murderous in Shanghai. At that time, it was simply a dark age, a terrible age, rarely seen in history. Sun Chuanfang and the others thought that this cruel policy of violence would definitely suppress the revolutionary forces and definitely re-stabilize their rule. But what was the fact? The old still declined, and the new still rose!

It is said that the times are different now. It is certainly not appropriate to talk much about things like resisting Japan and opposing imperialism. Even talking about personal matters of eating, such as how hard life is, etc., is said to be extremely dangerous. It is clear that we are suffering from unbearable oppression, but those oppressors insist that there is no such thing. It is clear that we should complain, we should cry out, but they simply don't allow you to complain, they simply don't allow you to cry out. Of course, many people simply don't listen to their words, insist on complaining, insist on crying out, and then they will move to cover your mouth, and they will:：：, to the point where they can't complain, can't cry out, and then stop.

In this way, the temporary victory at present seems to belong to them, but wait! What does history tell us? In fact, they have not gained any victory. All their efforts only prove that the tide of revolution has already reached the highest point, and their prosperous fate will also be completely overthrown in this last struggle. If you don't believe it, watch!

[L Special Self-Occupation Ji

An Unofficial History of Employment Agencies 281

— Dan Sheng

Chapter X: A Dead End - The Desperate Idiot Hopes for Collapse; Dan Fan Dances with Hunger and Seeks Refuge at an Employment Agency

It is said that Dan Fan Sheng heard the person next door lamenting to himself, "Rent, the landlord will be here again in two days to collect; rice, there's only enough for two more days of porridge; firewood money, I can't keep owing that at the end of the month. I really don't know why my father made me study these life-destroying books. Did he expect me to file lawsuits on the waterfront? If I die, what will happen to my family, the old and the young? I'd rather the heavens collapsed sooner so we can all die and be done with it! Heaven, are you going to collapse or not? How much longer are you going to torment us?"

Hearing this, Dan Fan Sheng found the man's madness laughable, but he himself was in the same boat. He couldn't laugh and was instead filled with his own troubles. He thought, three years ago, he was also a parasite in a high-ranking official's household. But because he saw his aging father using blood, sweat, and brains to earn money that was wasted on those young masters' entertainment, he felt it was not only worthless but also troubled his conscience. So, he steeled himself and abandoned the life of a "hotel" where he was reserved for a high-ranking position and went out to serve society. Although he was by nature foolish, he could still write ABCs and count 3x1=3 and 4x1=4. So, three months after joining the organization, he earned 45 dollars a month. Who knew the Japanese devils would come and destroy his ancestors! In order to economize and prepare for long-term resistance, he reduced expenses, the organization merged, and Dan Fan Sheng packed his bags and went back to his hometown to eat hometown rice. But blessings never come in pairs, and misfortunes never come alone. This year, his sixty-year-old father, who had worked at the shop for thirty years, was also affected by the situation and the shop closed down. His old parents, two younger siblings, and an older brother who had gone off to be an apprentice, all depended on him. Thinking of this, Dan Fan Sheng couldn't help but be infected by the person next door and also wished "the heavens would collapse sooner."

But afterward, Dan Fan Sheng understood that the heavens would not collapse. But solving the problems on his shoulders was almost like squeezing the juice out of his brain, and he couldn't think of an effective solution. Rely on friends? But his friends were also thinking of relying on friends. Find relatives? But his relatives were also looking to find relatives. It was truly "no way to go to heaven, no door to enter the earth." Suddenly, a light flashed in Dan Fan Sheng's eyes, and he thought of a glimmer of hope.

It turned out that Dan Fan Sheng remembered an old lady who was said to be sixty years old last year and was looking for something to do. She had opened an employment agency at 24 Hankou Road. She was kindhearted, and she didn't charge anyone she helped find employment. But he heard that the employment agency was small, and when it first opened, the old lady's room was almost broken down by the many eager applicants. Later, he heard that she was compassionate and opened up some space in her back room. But he didn't know if there was still room to accommodate later applicants.

Dan Fan Sheng didn't think about it anymore. He found half a sheet of white paper in the pile of broken books, picked up a writing brush, and wrote a line of "Big Sale" in three characters, and below it, he wrote, "Regardless of cost, half price, original price 45 dollars." Dan Fan Sheng knew that this year was a time of price reductions in all industries, so he stole this concept. After writing, he stuck it on his long gown, got on his two-wheeled vehicle, and rushed towards the employment agency. When he arrived at the door of the shop, he saw that it lived up to its reputation. The small shop was filled with a dark mass of people. Dan Fan Sheng tiptoed and saw that the proprietress, despite her age, was not spared any effort. She was standing on tiptoes, busy and happy. Dan Fan Sheng wiped the cold sweat on his forehead and stepped inside, not knowing how the proprietress would treat him. Listen to her own explanation in the next chapter.

Shen Bao Local Supplement - Film Supplement

New Atmosphere in the Australian Film Industry (Part 2) 282

— Shen Weng

Film giants realize the outflow of money

Join forces to organize large companies to resist imported products

Snowy Scene is currently producing a film called "The Squatter's Daughter," which describes the realities of life on a sheep station. This large sheep station is run by one person. Its area is about the same size as England. An English county can be placed in the corner of this large pasture. The film that is prepared to be produced next is called "The Silence of Dean Maitland." Its story is based on a famous novel and sets the background in a peaceful English village, where there are raging waves and fishing scenes. And the protagonists in the play are those vulgar and sincere villagers. Thus, all the secrets of Australia will be revealed on the screen.

Both of these films will be directed by Hall (Ken G. Hall), and Captain Frank Hurley will assist from the side. He is the director of photography for the world-famous Shackleton Antarctic Expedition. He once bet Shackleton that he would find the film that was washed away by the iceberg in the icy waters. As a result, Shackleton lost. He also flew in an airplane to the clouds of New Guinea to shoot a film.

In the near future, those strange films will be produced in Australia and its southern neighbors. Not long ago, a nephew of Sir Harry, who led the cavalry to conquer Palestine, went to Batukelu Island in the South Pacific to make a film. Two hundred miles from the coast, they fought a war with the natives in the turbulent ocean. As a result, they were captured from the ship by the natives. They stayed on the island for several weeks, where they lived with illegal thugs and Tahitian women. Although the purpose of filming was achieved, they escaped from the tiger's mouth on a passing ship on a dark night; but their lives were almost lost.

At this time, Monkeman's short film "The Great Barrier Reef" may be seen on the British screen. These reefs extend nearly a thousand miles along the coast of Queensland, parallel on both sides by man-eating sharks. If you wear Wellington boots and step onto the coral island, you will find many strange things. A sea snake pounces on you, and you will naturally jump elsewhere, but perhaps this jump will step on a stonefish. Good heavens! You can no longer tell whether it is an animal or a stone, but its sharp spines have already pierced into your foot. If you are a native from a trepang fishing boat, you are sure to die, but if you are a white man, it doesn't matter, because you are wearing boots!

In addition to this, there are many other rare and wonderful things that can be used as material for future Australian films. The difficulty now lies in the problem of talent. The role now needed is to be young and romantic. Mr. Serling has already discovered two, one is Leif Hicks, and the other is Cecil Scott. Although there are many other film talents, they have all gone to Elstree or Hollywood to test their fate.

In the next twelve months, more local actors may be seen to have an opportunity to develop; but for the time being, there is still a lack of talent. Snowy Scene Company will proceed with the production of "The Silence of Dean Maitland" and also prepare to go to England to find a star to play the leading role in Australia. Therefore, they should not only have a great organization for film companies; but also have to find ways to cultivate film talents. This is the current situation of the Australian film industry, which is quite an improvement compared to the past. (The End)

Film Reviews

Review of (Hot Pepper) 283

— Ling He

The plot is lively, the meaning is superficial

Both the direction and performance are worth seeing

Generally, people who are often close to American movies will know that American movies at present cannot escape the trap of "sensuality" or "glamour." Thus, this kind of picture full of golden colors has indeed become an intoxicating entertainment weapon for the owners of material civilization. If we still hope to obtain some works of great value in addition to this substance, of course, this will inevitably disappoint us.

Sure enough, American filmmakers are still trying their best to circle in this narrow range. However, in order to avoid complete similarity in each film, the directors or screenwriters have to change the plot of the film, and the entire content is, of course, consistent with other works. Regarding this point, we can see it in "Hot Pepper."

So, what is in Hot Pepper? There are hot girls, violent gentlemen, indulgent songs and dances, naked shivers, large amounts of drinking, and extravagant gambling. Fraud and intimidation to obtain wealth, selling smuggled goods to get rich, all of this is the reality of the upper class, but it is also an exposure of their sins. Of course, we cannot say that such content is meaningless, but it is obviously just an exposure.

In this film, there is a lively plot, from beginning to end, there is no dullness at all. Here, we can clearly know the efforts of director John Blystone. However, after watching this film, we cannot be stimulated in the slightest, so it cannot give us any deep impression. Of course, this is because it is limited to the form of comedy, but if the content can be more

Can be enriched, it can still affect the audience, right?

Several major actors who have already become famous, of course, are still no less than their past achievements. However, if Victor McLaglen's actions are monotonous, it will not be able to gain the full favor of the audience. The performance of Lupe Velez, who plays the hot girl Pepper, is indeed very vivid. Although her wild exposure is inevitably exaggerated, she fully develops the personality of the character in the play and gives the film a special color.

In short, in this film, we can see the characteristics of capitalist movies, and this is the phenomenon that should occur in the process of collapse.

Audience Opinions

The Characteristics of Jin Henry's "State Fair" 284

— Jie Ke

Jin Henry's "State Fair" is indeed a very lively and interesting film: one scene after another unfolds the plot, and one scene after another reflects the delicate and flexible vivid interest. The characters in the play, such as Janet Gaynor as the beautiful farm girl, Will Rogers as the cautious rich farmer, Sally Eilers as the affectionate actress, Lew Ayres as the young newspaper reporter, Lois Trancy as the rich farmer's wife, Norman Foster as the unwilling farm boy, all performed as very appropriate supporting roles.

The structure of this film takes an idyllic American rural life as its prelude; the annual state fair, which is now translated as the State Fair, is the backbone. People from cities and villages in each state come to participate in this State Fair, so there is naturally an opportunity to give birth to many interesting things. Finally, this film returns to the original rural family as its epilogue, but the ending scene of this film must give the beautiful farm girl and the young newspaper reporter a happy ending in a romantic story that happened at the State Fair.

Jin Henry's most successful point is being vivid, flexible in being vivid, and being interesting, in being different. This film can be said to be vivid and interesting in every scene, and its vivid interest comes from indirect and very natural sources. The most characteristic example is when the judges at the State Fair are judging, everyone is holding their breath and waiting for the results of the judgment. It should be as dull as death and not vivid. However, everyone is constantly shaking a fan together, and each person's fan is different in various ways. In this way, on the one hand, the heat of autumn at the time of the State Fair gathering is described, and on the other hand, this scene is made vivid. Furthermore, when the farm girl and the newspaper reporter are in love for the first time, and even later when they are whispering sweet words, they are all set off by a speeding car, which makes the quiet love process vivid and draws the color picture of the State Fair. The rest are like the night when the farm boy and the actress have a tryst and say goodbye. We can vaguely see a bed, and clearly hear the voices of the farm boy and the actress whispering sweet words. For several minutes, there is no one's movement, but there is the constant change of light and the leisurely floating of the gauze window blown by the breeze. Here it is vivid. Finally, when the newspaper reporter and the farm girl reunite after a farewell, it is raining heavily all day long. The two hug and kiss each other in the rustling rain, and the large advertising board of the State Fair along the road is used as the background. The raindrops wet the advertising paper, followed by the shattered fall of the few big characters of the State Fair on the advertising board, and this "State Fair" film also closed. How vivid! What flexible wrists!

The jokes in this film, some are borrowed from actions, and some are borrowed from words, and there are not a few of them. A white pig is angry because of love, and withers because it does not see the red sow; the rich farmer is wholeheartedly guarding the piglets; and when judging the piglets, the music team is playing loudly, and the three strangely shaped judges are solemnly introducing them;—this is a joke with satire. After the seven-day period of the State Fair is over, everyone packs up their boxes, dismantles the sheds, and the cars slowly start to move, and a desolate scene of the end of the grand event is vividly in sight—this is the sorrow after the excitement.

Lyceum will have a grand event 285

— Xing Zhi

Twelve people, including Edgar Wallace, a world-renowned drama expert, will appear on stage at the Lyceum Theatre in Shanghai to meet with the people of Shanghai. It is said that the date is set for May 9th to 13th, a total of five days, and the play to be performed is "The Case of the Frightened Lady," a script written by Edgar himself, and it is also the whole cast's best play.

Edgar's reputation has shaken Europe and the United States. The scripts he wrote have the style of Shakespeare. The plays he made are sung throughout the literary world, but he rarely appears on stage in person. This time he came to Shanghai for a tour, and the owner of Lyceum specially invited him to perform on stage. Edgar was very interested, so he agreed to perform for five days. It is expected that the traffic will be heavy on Maersilu Road, and there will be a grand occasion.

YMCA opens scientific and educational activity films 286

— Cheng Zhi

The local Christian YMCA has always been based on promoting learning, and recently, from May 6th to May 27th, it will screen scientific and educational activity films in four phases every Saturday at 7:30 pm at the Eight Immortals Bridge Clubhouse. The films to be screened on May 6th include Earth Research, Water Research, Air Research, and Slapstick Films. Those to be screened on the 13th include Mosquito Research and Life History, Fly Research, Ant Research, and Slapstick Films. Those to be screened on the 20th include Scenery such as Arctic Icebergs and the Rhine River, Volcano Research, and Scenery of Southern China. Those to be screened on the 27th include Current Research, Rubber Manufacturing Method, Sugar Manufacturing Method, Brass Mining, and Slapstick Films. All members of the association can enter for free. Non-members will be charged only a dime each time, and those who purchase four times together will only be charged two dimes.

The Cold-Faced Man Marries a Nurse 287

— Guang Yi

Pace Carten, the famous cold-faced comedian on the screen, divorced his wife, Nerita Wen (cousin of Numen Taven, who played Camille). Requested a divorce in California. However, California must wait until August of this year to end the case. Carten couldn't bear it, so he went to Mexico and married his new lover, Ms. Mei, first. Ms. Mei was originally a hospital nurse. Carten was hospitalized due to illness, and then love happened.

Ai Xia's "Madam's Own Story" 288

— You You

In the domestic film industry, Ai Xia's history is not long. Now her status is still below others, but in China's team of stars who mostly cannot write, she can actually write her own script, which is quite something to be proud of.

The script of "A Modern Woman" describes a modern lady whose thinking is very free and very thorough; but she can't escape the love barrier and falls in love with a newspaper reporter who is already married. She said to him, "I know you are married, you love your wife very much; but I don't care, I just ask if you love me." In this way, she loves him with all her heart and soul. Later, he lost his job, and because she wanted to help him, she stole a check from a fat merchant who was often pursuing her, and was imprisoned. This was her hard work, but who knew that the newspaper reporter would not understand her behavior. At that time, it happened that she had a friend in prison with her. She was persuaded by her friend and realized her mistake. When she was released from prison, she became a brand new revolutionary woman.—The director of this film is Mr. Li Pingqian, and the protagonist is Ai Xia herself.

After "A Modern Woman" was written, everyone said that it was Ai Xia's autobiography, because she often advocated that love should be thorough. We dare not decide whether it is "Madam's Own Story"; but "words are the voice of the heart", there must be some of her thoughts inside, right?

Hollywood Star Claws 289

— A Lin

Liliane Hawe, the petite, lively, and innocent singer and dancer in "Dragon Soaring Phoenix Dance," has been silent for a long time since she was recruited by Fox Company. Now she is co-starring with John Boles in "My Lips Betray." One has a melodious voice, and the other has a loud golden voice. Their cooperation is a perfect match! And this is also Ms. Hawe's post-remarriage debut!

George Raft, the second Valentino, is now a big star worshiped by women, so he is very dissatisfied with his salary of 750 yuan per week and has asked Paramount to increase his salary to 2,500 yuan, otherwise he would rather not do it and go to Europe. But the company has not necessarily agreed.

Janet Gaynor and her new screen partner, French star Henri Garat's collaboration "Adorable" is already in production, but her contract with Fox will expire in June, and many companies are willing to pay her a salary greater than 2,500 yuan, but she may not want to leave her place of origin, Fox!

Film Novel 42nd Street (Part 2) 290

— Si Ping

Dance leader Lee Andy deliberately pretended not to be embarrassed and talked to Ma Bu sideways. Pierre hurriedly jumped from the sound cotton team seat to Ma Xi's side.

"You don't have to wait, Mr. Ma Xi," Pierre interjected. "It just so happens that there is a girl here. And she is also a top dancer. I have been watching her all day. You have also seen her twice, but she was eliminated the third time."

When Andy led Pan Qi to the front of the stage, she was still half asleep, but Ma Xi's voice woke her up.

"She can do it," Ma Xi said after looking at her.

When Ma Xi was sitting alone in the room, Jones came.

"You naturally know that Abner Dillon is making trouble in the troupe," Jones said sternly. "Hey, what she likes about this troupe is Toresai Buick. He is afraid that he will withdraw his shares."

"Why?" Ma Xi replied hesitantly.

"Why, because Miss Buick is double-dealing right in front of him."

"With whom?" Ma Xi asked, showing concern for the first time.

"With a playmate from her playground. Now that she has come here to start another class, he has followed her. If Dillon finds out about this, he will definitely not do it, and then it will be terrible."

"What are you doing?" Jones asked suspiciously when Ma Xi reached out to make a phone call.

"I'm going to discuss it with my friend Mo Fei," Ma Xi replied. "He never likes playgrounds."

"Is it Shi Limo Fei?" Jones retorted. "You can't, Qiu Lin. Listen. I don't want to associate with gangsters like Mo Fei."

"Can't I?" Ma Xi retorted. "If anyone wants to destroy my dance troupe, I can't talk about what means to use to deal with them."

When Ma Xi was discussing with Mo Fei, Toresai and Pan Te were sitting side by side on a bench in Central Park Lake, entangled in love. Such an appointment was their only opportunity to express their love to each other.

Pan Te's arm was tightly around her, her head resting on her shoulder, and Toresai was completely intoxicated in the quick rush. But Pan Te was pondering.

"Let's not be children anymore, Tao," he said. "Your future is great. I always limit you, like hooking your neck. When people don't see me, I can only see you doing this secretly, which makes it difficult for me to be a human being. It doesn't sound good for a man to not do anything and take money from a woman, Tao."

"But my current position is entirely given to me by you, Pan." Toresai protested. "It was you who created my singing and dancing art. You trained me, guided me, told me everything, I have not forgotten." (To be continued)
